[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer-based fuzzing run against the Apache Commons Compress “Expander” example   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         triggered a critical security alert. The built-in FilePathTraversal sanitizer       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         detected a file path traversal when expanding an archive, causing                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal` [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to be thrown.                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue type: File path traversal vulnerability                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Trigger: During execution of `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`, the fuzzer supplied input    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         that led to a target file path escaping the intended extraction directory [1m([0me.g.,    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/tmp/[0m…[35m/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`[1m)[0m.                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Stack trace highlights:                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           - `[1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` in the Jazzer sanitizers library detected the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         unsafe path.                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           - Control flows through `[1;35mcheckPath[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` and `[1;35mcopyMismatchMvHook[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` in         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FilePathTraversal`.                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           - The vulnerability surfaces in the example code at                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` [1m([0mmultiple     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         overloads[1m)[0m and is invoked by the harness method                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mExpanderFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:52[0m[1m)[0m`.                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Important observations and findings:                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The alert originates from Jazzer’s sanitizer logic rather than a crash. It marks  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the input as an exploitable security issue [1m([0mpath traversal[1m)[0m.                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The file path traversal occurs during the archive-expansion routine, suggesting   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         that relative paths or crafted entries bypass checks and write outside the target   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory.                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The harness [1m([0mFuzzerTestOneInput[1m)[0m is the entry point for testing; it repeatedly    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         calls `Expander.expand` but is not itself the cause.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Areas for code review:                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The path-checking and sanitization logic in the Expander example:                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • All overloads of `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` in                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The handling of entry names and destination paths before file creation          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The `[1;35mcopyMismatchMvHook[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`, `[1;35mcheckPath[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`, and `[1;35mcheck[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` methods in      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` class to see how paths are validated and what edge     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         cases may slip through                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Any utility methods in Commons Compress that normalize or resolve entry names     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         prior to file system operations                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         This investigation will provide a holistic understanding of how archive entries are [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         processed and where path traversal defenses can be bolstered.                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer fuzz run on the Apache Commons Compress `Expander` example resulted in a[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace shows the standard library’s `FilePathTraversal.check` routines [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflagging an out-of-bounds extraction path when `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` writes archive [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries to disk.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This indicates that a crafted archive entry name or symlink target can escape the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended output directory.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `Expander.java`, around line [0m[1;36m471[0m[39m, the patch:  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Adds `final Path targetDirPath = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Replaces uses of `[0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with [0m                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Inserts `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mpath.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguards for both link and target paths in the symlink branch.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Mirrors this logic in the “non-directory” branch, declaring  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      `final Path target = [0m[1;35mtargetDirPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    then reassigning `target` later if the parent check fails.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The intent is to prevent zip-slip and symlink-based traversal by rejecting any [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry whose normalized path leaves the target directory.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During compilation, Maven reports:  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    `[0m[35m/src/commons-compress/src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/exam[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35mples/[0m[95mExpander.java[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m513[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m21[0m[1;39m][0m[39m cannot assign a value to final variable target`  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error arises because the patch marks `target` as `final` in the non-directory[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranch but includes code later that reassigns to `target`.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- As a result, the build fails and no corrected artifact is produced.[0m               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m470[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m520[0m[39m, where `target` and `link` are declared and potentially reassigned.  [0m [2m                [0m
